 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;2.02. Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On August&#160;5, 2021, iCAD, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release announcing its financial results for the quarter ended June&#160;30, 2021. A copy of the Company&#8217;s press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1. Exhibit 99.1 is being furnished pursuant to Item 2.02, is not to be considered filed under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), and shall not be incorporated by reference into any of the Company&#8217;s previous or future filings under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;9.01 Financial Statements and Exhibits. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) Exhibits </p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ICAD REPORTS FINANCIAL RESULTS FOR THE QUARTER ENDED JUNE&nbsp;30, 2021 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Conference Call Today at 4:30 PM ET </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>NASHUA, N.H. &#150; August</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;5, 2021 &#150;</B> iCAD, Inc. (NASDAQ: ICAD),&nbsp;a global medical technology leader providing innovative
cancer detection and therapy solutions, today reported its financial and operating results for the three and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Revenues for the three-month and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> periods ended June&nbsp;30, 2021 were $7.8&nbsp;million and
$16.5&nbsp;million, respectively, compared to $5.6&nbsp;million and $12.1&nbsp;million in the three and six month periods ended June&nbsp;30, 2020, respectively. Net loss for the three-month and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT>
periods ended June&nbsp;30, 2021 were $3.3&nbsp;million and $4.9&nbsp;million, respectively, compared to $2.4&nbsp;million and $14.2&nbsp;million in the three and six month periods ended June&nbsp;30, 2020, respectively. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Recent Highlights: </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Continued market penetration with ProFound AI&reg; Risk, the first and only commercially available clinical
decision support tool providing <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-year</FONT> breast cancer risk estimation personalized for each woman, for 2D mammography in the U.S. and Europe, with approximately 250 software licenses installed to date
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Showed continued strength in the Therapy business with $3&nbsp;million in revenues, which represents 3.8% growth
over a very strong first quarter, driven largely by the continued surge in dermatology controller installations reflecting positive shifts in market dynamics </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Signed a global distribution agreement with Sectra, a leading international medical imaging IT and cybersecurity
company, expanding access to ProFound AI &reg; and ProFound AI &reg; Risk to additional facilities and imaging centers worldwide </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

and faster processing time compared to the prior versions </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our second quarter total revenue was negatively impacted by longer than expected Enterprise sales cycles in several large prospective accounts. We began
to close some of these accounts in July. While we anticipate the longer Enterprise sales cycle will continue to be a meaningful component of our pipeline, the addition of these Enterprise sales will increase our addressable market and future average
deal size,&#148; said Mike Klein, Chairman and CEO. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We continue to be pleased with the performance of our Therapy segment. Total Therapy revenues
of $3&nbsp;million represented a 109% percent increase over the second quarter of last year and a 3.8% increase over a strong first quarter in 2021. This growth was primarily driven by dermatology controller installations, which are being heavily
influenced by the emergence of positive shifts in reimbursement, payor coverage and regulatory changes,&#148; concluded Mr.&nbsp;Klein. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Second Quarter
2021 Financial Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Total Detection and Therapy revenue for the second quarter of 2021 was $7.8&nbsp;million, an increase of $2.3&nbsp;million, or
41%, as compared to the second quarter of 2020. </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Revenue: Cancer Detection revenue for the second quarter of 2021, which includes the Company&#146;s
mammography and breast density products, and the associated service and supplies revenue, increased by approximately $0.7&nbsp;million, or 16%, to $4.8&nbsp;million, as compared to the second quarter of 2020. Therapy revenue for the second quarter
of 2021, which includes Xoft<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Axxent&reg; eBx<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> System<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> sales, as well as the
associated service and supplies revenue, increased by $1.6&nbsp;million, or 109%, to $3.0&nbsp;million, as compared to the second quarter of 2020. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

$4.4&nbsp;million, or 78% of revenue, in the second quarter of 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating Expenses: Total operating expenses for the second quarter of 2021 were
$8.4&nbsp;million, a $1.7&nbsp;million, or 26% increase from $6.7&nbsp;million in the second quarter of 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GAAP Net Loss: Net loss for the second
quarter of 2021 was ($3.3) million, or ($0.13) per diluted share, as compared to a net loss of ($2.4) million, or ($0.11) per diluted share, for the second quarter of 2020. GAAP Net Loss in 2021 included a $0.4&nbsp;million charge related to the
losses on the extinguishment of debentures and debt. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss:
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss, a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure as defined below, for the second quarter of 2021 was ($2.8) million, or ($0.11) per diluted share, as compared
to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss of ($2.5) million, or ($0.12) per diluted share, for the second quarter of 2020. Please refer to the section entitled &#147;Reconciliation of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures&#148; and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss results for the three-month periods ended June&nbsp;30, 2021 and 2020, respectively. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA, a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure as defined below, for the second quarter of 2021 was a
loss of ($2.1) million, a ($1.4) million increased loss as compared to the second quarter 2020 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA loss of ($0.7) million. Please refer to the section entitled &#147;Reconciliation of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures&#148; and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA results for the three-month periods ended June&nbsp;30, 2021 and 2020, respectively. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Six Months Ended June&nbsp;30, 2021 Financial Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Total Detection and Therapy revenue for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2021 was $16.5&nbsp;million, an increase of $4.4&nbsp;million, or 36%, as compared
to the same period in 2020. </P>

to $8.9&nbsp;million, or 73% of revenue, in the same period in 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating Expenses: Total operating expenses for the six months ended June&nbsp;30,
2021 were $16.2&nbsp;million, a $1.1&nbsp;million, or 7.6%, increase from $15.1&nbsp;million in the same period in 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GAAP Net Loss: Net loss for the
six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2021 was ($4.9)&nbsp;million, or ($0.20) per diluted share, as compared to a net loss of ($14.2)&nbsp;million, or ($0.67) per diluted share, for the same period in 2020. GAAP Net Loss in 2020 included a
$7.5&nbsp;million charge related to the losses on fair value of convertible debentures. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net
Loss: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss, a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure as defined below, for the first half of 2021 was ($4.4)&nbsp;million, or ($0.18) per diluted share, as
compared to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss of ($6.4) million, or ($0.30) per diluted share, for the first half of 2020. Please refer to the section entitled &#147;Reconciliation of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures&#148; and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss results for the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> periods ended June&nbsp;30, 2021 and 2020, respectively. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA, a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure as defined below, for the first half of 2021 was a loss of ($2.6) million, a $1.2&nbsp;million decrease as compared to the first half 2020 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP
Measures </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company reports its financial results in accordance with United States generally accepted accounting principles, or GAAP. However,
management believes that in order to understand the Company&#146;s short-term and long-term financial and operational trends, investors may wish to consider the impact of certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> or <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> items, when used as a supplement to financial performance measures in accordance with GAAP. These items result from facts and circumstances that vary in frequency and/or impact on continuing
operations. Management also uses results of operations before such items to evaluate the operating performance of the Company and compare it against past periods, make operating decisions, and serve as a basis for strategic planning. These <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provide management with additional means to understand and evaluate the operating results and trends in the Company&#146;s ongoing business by eliminating certain <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> expenses and other items that management believes might otherwise make comparisons of the Company&#146;s ongoing business with prior periods more difficult, obscure trends in ongoing operations or reduce
management&#146;s ability to make useful forecasts. Management believes that these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provide additional means of evaluating period-over-period operating performance. In addition,
management understands that some investors and financial analysts find this information helpful in analyzing the Company&#146;s financial and operational performance and comparing this performance to its peers and competitors. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management defines <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA&#148; as the sum of GAAP Net Loss before provisions for interest
expense, other income, stock-based compensation expense, depreciation and amortization, tax expense, severance, gain on sale of assets, loss on disposal of assets, acquisition and litigation related expenses. Management considers this <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure to be an indicator of the Company&#146;s operational strength and performance of its business and a good measure of its historical operating trends, in particular the extent to which
ongoing operations impact the Company&#146;s overall financial performance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures do
not replace the presentation of the Company&#146;s GAAP financial results and should only be used as a supplement to, not as a substitute for, the Company&#146;s financial results presented in accordance with GAAP. The Company has provided a
reconciliation of each <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure used in its financial reporting and investor presentations to the most directly comparable GAAP financial measure. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management excludes each of the items identified below from the applicable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure referenced above
for the reasons set forth with respect to that excluded item: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Interest expense: The Company excludes interest expense which includes interest from the facility agreement,
interest on capital leases and interest on the convertible debentures from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA calculation. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

that management does not consider part of ongoing operating results when assessing the performance of the Company&#146;s business, and also because the total amount of expense is partially outside of the Company&#146;s control as it is based on
factors such as stock price volatility and interest rates, which may be unrelated to our performance during the period in which the expense is incurred. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

periods as it was not considered by management in making operating decisions, and management believes that such item does not have a direct correlation to future business operations. In January 2021, the Company adopted ASU <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2019-12</FONT> requiring these taxes be moved to operating expenses and are no longer excluded. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

generally cannot be changed or influenced by management after they are acquired. Accordingly, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items are not considered by management in making operating decisions, and management believes that
such expenses do not have a direct correlation to future business operations. Thus, including such charges does not accurately reflect the performance of the Company&#146;s ongoing operations for the period in which such charges are incurred.
